triggers {
  name: "MapSetup"
  events {
    ops {
      functionName: "On Map Setup"
    }
  }
  conditions {
  }
  actions {
    ops {
      functionName: "Set Environmental Effect Amount"
      args {
        call_value {
          functionName: "Get Preset Value (string)"
          args {
            string_value: "EnvironmentalEffects"
          }
          args {
            int_value: 0
          }
        }
      }
      args {
        int_value: 150
      }
    }
  }
  isActive: true
  idRef {
    id: "593781463565641040000267"
  }
  elseActions {
  }
  is_oneshot: true
}
